        <condition><![CDATA[if (Strcmp(Translate(Config_Options, true, "CreateNewClassificationValue", "Bloomberg_DL_Credit_Risk"), "YES"))
	if (Strcmp(ERRORCODE, "0") && OneHasValue(INDUSTRY_SUBGROUP, INDUSTRY_SECTOR, INDUSTRY_GROUP, OBLIG_INDUSTRY_SUBGROUP))
		return "INCL";
	else
		return "";
else if (Strcmp(Translate(Config_Options, true, "CreateNewClassificationValue", "Bloomberg_DL_Credit_Risk"), "NO"))
	return "";
else if (!OneOf("NO", Translate(Config_Options, true, "CreateNewClassificationValue", "Bloomberg_DL_Credit_Risk"),
		"YES"))
	return ThrowMapError(
			Strcat(Translate(Config_Options, true, "CreateNewClassificationValue", "Bloomberg_DL_Credit_Risk"),
					Strcat("--",
							"Wrong value in Config_Option against Bloomberg_DL_Credit_Risk for CreateNewClassificationValue. It is other than permitted value YES, NO and No value used in Config_option")),
			"");
else
	return "";]]></condition>
        <Node name="MESSAGECONDITION" type="attribute">
          <expr><![CDATA[if (Strcmp(Translate(Config_Options, true, "CreateNewClassificationValue", "Bloomberg_DL_Credit_Risk"), "YES"))
	if (Strcmp(ERRORCODE, "0") && OneHasValue(INDUSTRY_SUBGROUP, INDUSTRY_SECTOR, INDUSTRY_GROUP))
		return "INCL";
	else
		return "";
else if (Strcmp(Translate(Config_Options, true, "CreateNewClassificationValue", "Bloomberg_DL_Credit_Risk"), "NO"))

        <comment><![CDATA[to take care of situation were we are getting the second last ultimate parent.]]></comment>

If we use, 'FINSCentralCrossReference', then FINS becomes its parent and when it is not able to find FINS (institution mnemonic), it throws an error.]]></comment>
